¬†The Spirit of Light!? Does that mean he‚Äôs related to¬†_those_¬†people I know?

In truth, I‚Äôm acquainted with several beings known as Spirits.

Napalm, the Fire Spirit.

BlastHole, the Earth Spirit.

Harp, the Wind Spirit.

WaterJet, the Water Spirit.

All of them are existences far beyond humanity, encountered at the end of various adventures across the lands. However, I‚Äôd heard there were six types of Spirits in total: the four elements‚ÄĒEarth, Water, Fire, and Wind‚ÄĒplus Light and Darkness.

I knew there were Spirits I hadn't met yet, but...

"Are you saying you're the Spirit of Light from among the Six Spirits?" I asked the radiance that had suddenly descended.

The thing glowed with an obnoxious intensity, as if to say,¬†_'Great beings are supposed to look sparkly, you know!'_¬†Still, though its outline was hazy, it seemed to take a humanoid form. In that regard, it was just like the others. Basic Spirit biology: a dense collection of fire, air, or whatever, shaped like a person. This fact supported its claim.

"But... if that's true...!?"

It called itself¬†Photon, the Spirit of Light. Which meant the god worshipped by the Photon Cult‚ÄĒthe ones currently giving me so much trouble‚ÄĒwas... this guy?

"A Spirit... calling itself a God!?"¬†

**_"Is that strange? We Spirits are the incarnations of Great Nature, supernatural beings who wield its raging power. Is that not exactly what you humans call a 'God'?"_**¬†

"Maybe, but..."

Still, this Spirit of Light, Photon, felt "off" compared to the elemental Spirits I'd met before. The others generally had no interest in human affairs and kept their distance, dwelling in unexplored regions or demonic lands where a lapse in focus meant instant death.

But this Light Spirit... it calls itself a 'God,' has built a whole organization of people to worship it, and seems actively involved in human society. On paper, that sounds helpful, but the reality?

**_"Sao, King of Light."_**¬†

"Yes?" What‚Äôs with that title? I have absolutely no memory of being called that.

**_"First, I shall bestow this upon you. Receive it with gratitude."_**

A thin beam of light shot from the Spirit. It looked like a laser, and since getting hit by a mysterious laser usually ends badly, I instinctively flipped away to dodge it.

**_"Do not dodge! This is a noble and holy gift!"_**¬†

"You can't just say that and expect me to stand still!?"

I stay cautious around things I don't understand. But since the Spirit was making such a scene, I stood still and accepted it the second time. The laser hit my chest, carving a pattern into my skin.

"Could this be...!?"¬†**_"_**

**_Heh, so you've noticed. I suppose you would, having already collected four crests from the lower Spirits."_**

A pure white crest now glowed on my pectoral.

**_"This is the 'Light Stigma,' the proof of one recognized by the Spirit of Light! With this, you bear the mark of a Holy Hero acknowledged by the God of Light!"_**

That said, my chest was already decorated with crests glowing in crimson, gold, deep green, and aqua blue. With white added to the mix, I was looking pretty colorful. I‚Äôm basically¬†Gaming Sao.

These were proof of recognition from the Spirits I'd met previously. They were incredibly useful items that allowed the bearer to manifest a portion of the Spirit‚Äôs power at will.

"But why give it so easily?"

From what I‚Äôd heard, a Spirit‚Äôs crest was a legendary treasure given only to those the Spirit truly took a liking to. It was a coveted power boost. I'd even met people who tried to enslave Spirits just to obtain that power. That‚Äôs how rare and terrifying these marks were.

So, for the Spirit of Light to just hand it over... is he a nice guy? Or a nice Spirit?

**_"Kuhahaha... Do you not understand? My inner thoughts?"_**

Correction. This guy definitely has an ulterior motive. That laugh is disgusting.

**_"I have heard the rumors on the wind. Or in my case, rumors on the light?"_**¬†

"Who cares? Get to the point."

**_"Regardless, a human who has gathered all four crests of the lower Spirits has appeared for the first time in ages. While the four elements are lower in rank than the Spirit of Light, they still hold great power within nature. Having gathered them all, it is no exaggeration to say that though you are human, you have become an incarnation of nature itself."_**¬†

"If you say so..." I honestly didn't fully get it myself.

**_"That is why you are worthy of being chosen by me. As my first servant, you are fit to fill the world with the Will of Light."_**¬†

"Hm?"¬†

**_"Sao, King of Light. What do you think of this world?"_**

Oh boy, here it comes. The "the world is rotten so I'm going to innovate it" monologue typical of high-concept villains. Usually, it's just edgy types who try way too hard to use big words...

**_"From my perspective as a Transcendent, this world is far too incomplete. Humans who cannot control their emotions, monsters running rampant... this world needs someone to unite everything and lead it correctly. Who do you think is suited for that?"_**¬†

"Are you going to say 'yourself'?"¬†

**_"Exactly! As expected of the King of Light I have chosen!"_**

I‚Äôd be more surprised if there were any other candidate after a setup like that. The level of self-affirmation is terrifying.

**_"Regrettably, the other Spirits are indifferent to the governance of the world. Because they are incarnations of nature, they believe that things are correct 'as they are.' But I am different. This is starting to sound like a shady self-help seminar.

**_"That is why I established the Photon Cult to worship me as a God and have guided my followers. But it is not enough. My grand ambition is to lead every human in the world. My followers still account for less than a tenth of all humanity!"_**¬†

"I see." That‚Äôs plenty, dude. Have you ever heard of 'diversity'?

"Uh-huh." Seriously, what is with that 'King of Light' title? Is it some cringey chuunibyou name?

Come to think of it, I remember someone saying something like that. ‚ÄĒ_'He who receives the crests of all six Spirits shall become the King of the World.'_¬†I thought it was just an urban legend, but coming from a Spirit's mouth, it has some weight.

**_"Then, you shall exercise your authority as King of the World and make every human on Earth join the Photon Cult! You are the first servant of the God of Light!!"_**¬†

"Eeeeh."¬†

**_"With this, the world shall be perfect! Every living thing shall worship and revere Photon, the God of Light! That is a perfect world! And I shall be revered for eternity in that perfect world! I, Photon, the Spirit and God of Light!"_**

"Punch."

**_"Gubeh!?"_**

I punched the Spirit right in the face. It actually worked‚ÄĒthe Spirit of Light took the fist to the cheek and went spinning through the air.

**_"Onga-gogo-gueeeeeeee!? What!? What was that!?"_**

"The cult that worships you? I flatly refuse. Joining something like that isn't going to make anyone happy or peaceful."

Actually, I can see exactly what would happen: a total surveillance society. Those who worship the Light God are favored; those who don't are persecuted. That‚Äôs just a straight-up dystopian nightmare. Did you really think I‚Äôd agree to that? Give me a break!

"I told your underlings already, but I recognize freedom of religion. I am firmly opposed to your plot to steal that freedom, and I will stop you! Even if I have to fight you right here!"

**_"Uguooooo...! It seems a mere human has gotten cocky! Did you think you could defy the Spirit of Light and get away with it!? It seems you need 'training.' I shall toy with you, break you, and show you that humans cannot win against Spirits before turning you into my loyal slave!"_**

If things don't go your way, use force. You really are a textbook villain. In that case, I have a counter-strategy. Unjust invasion shall not be forgiven!

**_"Fool! Do not think a human can defeat a Spirit just because they've received a little divine protection! Remember that the source of your power is us Spirits! Your power is merely a fraction of the Spirit power we lent you! There is no way you can defeat the Spirit itself, the source who can control one hundred percent of that power‚ÄĒAAAAAAGH!!"_**

"Flame Punch."¬†

**_"Gubeh!?"_**¬†

"Earth Kick."¬†

**_"Angoh!?"_**¬†

"Wind Submission."¬†

**_"Idadadadadada!?"_**¬†

"Water Splash."¬†

**_"Agyaaaaaaaaa!!"_**

I pummeled the Spirit of Light with a barrage of attacks. You‚Äôre the one who forgot something, buddy. The Spirit crests I have aren't just yours. I have the crests and powers granted by the Spirits of Earth, Water, Fire, and Wind.

**_"Guboh...? Impossible! Even if you have the crests of the four Spirits, the power they lend you should only be a tiny fraction. It shouldn't be nearly enough to defeat the God of Light, Photon, who is the Spirit itself!"_**

"You're right, normally. But something strange has been happening for a minute now."

**_"What!?"_**

Ever since we started, the power gushing out of my four elemental crests has been incomparable to anything before. It's on a whole different level.

"I bet the other Spirits are watching what‚Äôs happening here, aren't they?"¬†

**_"Wh...!?"_**¬†

"And they probably felt a sense of crisis regarding what you're doing, so they're lending me all their power just for now so I can stop you. That‚Äôs what it feels like."

Also, Spirit of Light. You kept calling the four elemental Spirits 'lower spirits' and talking down to them, didn't you? They probably heard that loud and clear. I can feel a non-insignificant amount of 'anger' mixed into the Spirit power erupting through me.

"I feel like they're telling me something. 'Beat the crap out of this idiot in our place'..."

**_"Hawawa...!? Wait, wait. Let's talk this out...!?"_**

"We'll talk. Right after I finish pounding you into the dirt."

**_"I'm telling you I'll make you the King of the World! Everything will be as you wish! You can hold any woman you want at any time! You like women, don't you!? If you become the slave of this Spirit of Light, anything...!!"_**

You really don't get it at all.

First, I can pretty much get my way without your permission. I‚Äôve got power from plenty of other Spirits, you see.

Second, 'hold any woman I want'? I can already do that. And it's not because of 'Royal Authority' or some other nonsense. Sex feels good because I like the woman, and she likes me, and then we join our genitals. What‚Äôs the point if it's forced through power?

I can't leave the world to someone who doesn't even understand that. I‚Äôll blast you away with the power the four Spirits lent me!

"Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind!!"

**_"Gurobogueeeeeeeeee!!"_**

The Spirit of Light was sent flying high into the sky by a barrage of punches infused with the power of the four elements.

# **162 - The Final Element**

"Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind!!"

The execution rush showed no signs of stopping.

The properties of the four elemental spirits were packed into every single punch. With hundreds of hits being hammered in at super-high speeds, not even a fellow spirit could expect to walk away unscathed after taking that kind of heat.

"Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind!!"

The Spirit of Light had initially maintained a humanoid silhouette, but after being subjected to such a relentless pummeling, it had been reduced to a wretched, unrecognizable heap, like a lump of clay mauled by a toddler.

But I didn't let up. As a finishing touch, I decided to treat it to the power of the "Light Stigma" I had just received from it.

"LIGHT!!‚ÄĒ"

And immediately, the four-element rush resumed!

"Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind-Earth-Water-Fire-Wind!!"¬†

**_"Yadda-baaaaa-gyaaaaaa‚ÄĒ!?"_**

The target was screaming nonsensical death throes from the sheer volume of trauma.

Alright, I‚Äôm starting to get bored. Time for the final blow! Take this‚ÄĒone last hit with every fiber of my being.

"Drop dead!!"¬†

**_"Gu-bugh!"_**

I slammed a final punch, infused with all the spirit power I possessed plus my own skills, and sent it flying.

It soared like a home-run ball, eventually colliding with the wall and making a disgusting¬†_splat_¬†sound.

Execution time: over.

"What was that...?"¬†

"The God of Light? No way...!"

The naked women present watched the scene unfold, completely dazed. They were the priestesses and followers of the Photon Cult. After demanding my conversion, they had been hit by a counter-offensive that turned them into my personal pleasure-slaves‚ÄĒhence their current lack of clothing.

I‚Äôd almost forgotten, but the Spirit of Light had descended right after our harem session. Most of them had been knocked out by the intense pleasure, but they were starting to wake up now, realizing the gravity of the situation.

Yes, ladies, that glowing pile of mincemeat over there is your god.

**_"Curse you... such tyranny against a god...!"_**

Oh, it's still alive. The Spirit of Light struggled to its feet, looking like a discarded rag.

**_"I thought I could rule the surface in a single stroke by using you, but I cannot leave such a dangerous existence unchecked... I cannot permit someone who wields the spirits' power and harbors clear rebellion against me to exist...!"_**

It muttered its villainous tropes under its breath.

**_"So be it! I shall use my full power to erase you! Even if the world is destroyed as collateral! First, with a Big Bang, this world and everything in it shall v‚ÄĒguebu!?"_**

It was saying some pretty high-stakes stuff, but the speech was never finished.

Because a massive mass of darkness crushed the light into the floor.

That might sound confusing, but I‚Äôm just describing exactly what happened. To be more specific: a single black point appeared in mid-air, expanded instantly, and manifested as a colossal block of pure shadow.

The light had no defense. It was swallowed and crushed instantly. The Spirit of Light was pinned down like Sun Wukong under the Five Elements Mountain... yet it still managed to shriek pathetically.

**_"Gueeee!? No... you!? Why here, why now!?"_**¬†

**_"You speak of folly. It is ordained that I manifest in this world when a King of the World is born."_**

The expanding darkness contracted, stopping once it had formed a humanoid shape.

A man of pure black.

His appearance, and that majestic aura I‚Äôd felt so many times before, gave it away instantly.

"The Dark Spirit...!?"¬†

**_"Indeed. Having met the others, your intuition is sharp. I am the leader and ruler of the Six Spirits: the Dark Spirit, Dark Matter."_**

The man of shadow spoke. To have another spirit show up while I was mid-fight with the first one... what brings you to my neck of the woods?

**_"I am Darkness. Darkness is the source from which all is born and the end to which all returns. Thus, I have no business in this manifest world where all things boast of life. There is no reason for me to appear here, save for an extremely rare exception."_**¬†

"But you're here right now, aren't you?"¬†

**_"Precisely because that rare exception has occurred. Five spirits, excluding myself, have granted their crests to a single individual."_**

... Oh, that's me.

**_"Therefore, I must judge for myself. Whether a hero has appeared who is worthy of receiving my final crest, the 'Origin Stigma,' and thus obtaining the crests of all spirits. Whether a hero has appeared who can have the world at his feet and change the very nature of existence."_**¬†**_"W-wait, my brother! This man is not fit to be King!"_**

The Spirit of Light, still pinned by the darkness, pleaded desperately.

**_"He lacks respect for us spirits! He beat me‚ÄĒthe incarnation of Light‚ÄĒto a pulp! If you give someone like that the authority of a King, our very existence will be at risk!"_**¬†**_"That is only because you are evil."_**¬†**_"GYAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA‚ÄĒ!!"_**

The darkness expanded, crushing the Spirit of Light even further.

**_"For a spirit to be consumed by greed and seek to influence the world of men is the height of vulgarity. To block and stop such a thing is a heroic act. He merely exercised the rights of a living being. It just so happens that the evil to be struck down was you."_**¬†

**_"_****_No! Ugehhhhh!?"_**¬†

**_"In any case, it was inevitable that I would appear once the fifth crest was granted. You should have known you would be dealt with right then and there. You are a pitiable, short-sighted worldling."_**¬†

**_"Ugehhhhhh!!"_**

The light was further pulverized by the dark.

From the looks of it, the Dark Spirit wasn't our enemy. It was just the Spirit of Light that was a weird, humanity-hating outlier.

**_"This fool, Photon, is one of our kind. I apologize for his misconduct. I promise to take him back to the multi-dimension where I reside and ensure he never interferes with this world again."_**¬†

**_"I don't want to goooo! I'm going to turn this world into a utopia that praises meeeeee!!"_**

It seems both humans and spirits have their share of troublemakers.

**_"However, my reason for appearing is not to judge this idiot. I have come to the manifest world for the first time in tens of millions of years for a much more important task."_**¬†

"To give me your crest... right?"¬†

**_"More accurately, to judge whether I should give you the crest."_**

It seemed the Dark Spirit held a special position even among the Six. The "Spirit King"‚ÄĒthat was the impression he gave.

**_"We spirits are nature itself... the embodiment of the world. To be granted our power means a human becomes one with nature and the world. To be recognized by all six spirits means a single personality can now bend the entire world to his will."_**¬†

"Isn't that... kind of a huge deal?"¬†

**_"You think so? It is preferable that the one who is to become King of the World takes the fact seriously."_**

He's talking about me, right!?

I already had five crests. And the sixth was standing right in front of me. This wasn't just a possibility anymore; I was one step away from ruling the world. Checkmate.

**_"The authority gained by completing the set of six crests far exceeds human imagination. Even the title 'King of the World' is too mild."_**

The Dark Spirit began to explain.

**_"You would control the world and nature. If you wished, you could dismantle this world and rebuild it from scratch. You could refresh the laws of nature. You could reconfigure the world exactly as you please."_**

So, less like a King and more like a¬†Game Master. If I got this crest, I would become an absolute being capable of manipulating the world at will. That was why the King of Niosebuk and his son Gangastra had been so desperate to find the spirits.

I‚Äôm glad they never got the power. Though, considering the Spirit King comes down to judge the final candidate, they probably never would have passed the test anyway.

**_"Tell me, Sao. Do you not wish to complete the Six Crests and become the ruler of the world?"_**

He asked it point-blank.

**_"You like women, do you not? The omnipotence gained from the Six Crests is incomparable to royal power. You could erase every other man from this world and monopolize every woman for yourself."_**

I guess if you can do whatever you want as a Game Master, that‚Äôs a given.

**_"You could ignore distance and time, holding every woman in the world simultaneously. And every child born from you would be female. If you interfere with causality using spirit power, you can manipulate the gender of your children at will."_**

Then I could plow the girls born from me, get them pregnant, and plow the daughters born from them... a cycle that continues for eternity.

**_"Immortality is a given once you complete the crests. You would drown in a never-ending sea of carnal desire. Is that not the ultimate wish of man? My 'Origin Stigma' can make that ideal a reality. What will you do?"_**

"I refuse."

Seriously, this has "trap" written all over it. They say there's no such thing as a free lunch. It was obvious I was being tested to see if I‚Äôd be blinded by power and run off to satisfy my own greed.

Too bad for him. I know plenty of stories and manga from my previous life; I know exactly how greedy people end up. I‚Äôm not picking the big gift box, and I‚Äôm not playing the role of the mean old man!

"Besides, even if I could become omnipotent, I'd pass on the future you described."¬†

**_"Oh?"_**

One man in the world, monopolizing all women. If you spend eternity just having sex like that, it stops being sex‚ÄĒit just becomes a task or a natural phenomenon. Where's the fun in that?

Sex is ultimately a reproductive act to leave descendants, but as humans developed hearts and emotions through evolution, sex gained a variety of meanings. It's an act to confirm love, or to show off one's ability by winning over an exceptional woman. It can be a vent for twisted emotions, a form of communication, or a way to establish a relationship. The more complex society gets, the more meaning sex has.

If you don't enjoy all of that combined, it's not sex. I don't want to strip away the wonderful meaning of sex just to be driven by my beastly urges.

"Besides, to truly enjoy sex, everyone has to be happy."¬†

**_"What do you mean by that?"_**

If it's not "All Happy," I can't enjoy it. There's sex in the world that involves force or NTR, making someone miserable. But I can't enjoy that. If the thought that my sex is making someone else miserable flickers in my mind, I can't devote myself to it fully.

Setting aside the trash who deserve to be miserable, if the world is a place where honest, innocent people are rewarded, then I can enjoy sex without any hesitation. That was exactly why I destroyed Niosebuk.

"Using the crests the way you suggested wouldn't make anyone happy. If that's the case, there's no point in having omnipotent power."

If I were to obtain that power... I‚Äôd want to use it so everyone in this world could live with a smile. Fun sex only exists when there's a smile to go with it.

...Oh, but I'd still use a snap of my fingers to turn playboys, thugs, and creepy old men into dust.

**_"Hehe... interesting."_**

The Dark Spirit seemed satisfied with my answer.

**_"If you had sought only your own greed here, I would have confiscated all your crests. In the process, your personality would have been dragged out, leaving you a vegetable."_**

I knew it was a trap! Don't make me walk across such a dangerous bridge without telling me, you bastard.

**_"And your answer was quite intriguing. Very well. I shall grant you my 'Origin Stigma.' Use the power of the spirits to try and build a world where everyone can live with a smile."_**

Well, to be more accurate... a world where everyone can have sex with a smile.

# **Epilogue**

In conclusion...

Even after receiving all six Spirit Crests, nothing much really changed.

That‚Äôs because my ideal had already been largely realized long before that.

A world where everyone can have sex with a smile.

I completely annihilated the Kingdom of Niosebuk, which threatened the peace, and for the time being, the scumbags who killed without reason or raped women have died out. In their place, I've built a new Autonomous Region, and little by little, I‚Äôm making it a better place to live.

Of course, I‚Äôm having a hell of a lot of sex at the same time.

There is only one reason why I make the world a better place.

It is so that I can have incredible sex.

To me, sex is the primary objective. To ensure that everyone can have sex that is pleasurable, comfortable, and fun, I continue to pour every ounce of my power into it today.

From here on out... And until the day I die...

I will use the wisdom and power of my reincarnation into this parallel world for one thing, and one thing only: to keep on having sex.

# **Afterword**

"I will use the wisdom and power of my reincarnation into this parallel world for one thing, and one thing only: to keep on having sex."

With that, this story comes to an end. Thank you very much for staying with me until the very finish.

I also apologize for the long wait; quite a lot of time passed after the temporary hiatus.

This work was a project where I aimed to create the most erotic content within the limits of my imagination, while also attempting to incorporate the standard tropes of "Narou" (Let's Become a Novelist) web novels.

To put it more simply, I wrote this thinking, "Wouldn't it be great if I could just do whatever lewd things I wanted within the template of an Isekai reincarnation story?"

I am truly happy that the readers accepted it, allowing the series to reach number one in the rankings and even receive a physical book publication.

The manga adaptation is also moving forward behind the scenes (as of October 2022), so I look forward to your continued support when that is officially announced.

As for my next endeavor, I‚Äôm interested in challenging myself with something different from novels in the realm of erotic content. I‚Äôm not sure yet if it will take a solid shape, but if we happen to cross paths elsewhere, I look forward to seeing you then.

Once again, thank you so much for reading this far.

Let‚Äôs meet again somewhere!
